<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">加行故者，謂如有一，由極猛利貪瞋癡纏，及極猛利無貪、無瞋、無癡加行，發起諸業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由加行的原因成猛利極重業，是指如有一類人，由於極為猛利的貪瞋癡煩惱現行，及極為猛利的無貪、無瞋、無癡善心加行，發起強而有力的惡行或善行造作種種的業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、串習</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科串習，由串習使業增上。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="09p648"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">串習故者，謂如有一，於長夜中，親近、修習、若多修習不善善業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由串習的原因成猛利極重業，是指如有一類人，在漫漫的無明長夜中，親近、修習、若多修習不善業或善業。夜是譬喻無明，無明相猶如黑暗的夜晚，有情的無明是無始以來就有的，稱為長夜。無始劫來，親近這種善業或不善業，第一次親近，接下來修習，常常這樣作，而且還不斷相續這樣作，就會變成猛利極重；學習佛法也是一樣，一次一次的學，學了一遍不夠再學一遍。這樣的業會使所造的業，變成猛利極重，就會很有力量。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、自性2　午一、依不善業辨</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科自性，由業自性使業增上，分二科；第一科依不善業辨，依不善業說明。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">自性故者，謂於綺語，麤惡語為大重罪；於麤惡語，離間語為大重罪；於離間語，妄語為大重罪。於欲邪行，不與取為大重罪；於不與取，殺生為大重罪。於貪欲，瞋恚為大重罪；於瞋恚，邪見為大重罪。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於業本身的自性成猛利極重業方面，先說不善業，是指相對於綺語，麤惡語是大而重的罪；相對於麤惡語，離間語是大而重的罪；相對於離間語，妄語為大而重的罪。相對於欲邪行，不與取為大而重的罪；相對於不與取，殺生為大而重的罪。相對於貪欲，瞋恚為大而重的罪；相對於瞋恚，邪見為大而重的罪。業本身的體性稱為自性，業的自性有輕有重，因此十惡業也是有輕有重。身三語四，是前重於後，於身業中殺生是最重的；貪瞋等三，邪見是最重的，因為邪見會生生世世廣為影響多數人。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、依善業辨2　未一、於三褔事</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科依善業辨，依善業說明業增上，分二科；第一科於三福事，於布施、持戒及修四無量心三福使業增上。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又於施性，戒性無罪為勝；於戒性，修性無罪為勝。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依善業的施、戒、修三福事作比較，相對於布施，持戒比布施還要殊勝一點。布施有時候心裡還充滿著種種的期望，希望回報，或者是貪瞋癡煩惱也沒有降伏，與持戒比起來，持戒的人不造惡的，所以持戒比布施還要殊勝。持戒與修定相比，修禪定（四無量心）還注意調伏內心的煩惱，因此修定比持戒還要更殊勝，所以修性無罪為勝。佛法很注重有沒有罪，罪是由那裡來？是由貪瞋癡來的。所以注意調伏內心的貪瞋癡，是佛法的重點。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、於三慧事</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科於三慧事，由聞、思、修使業增上。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於聞性，思性無罪為勝；如是等。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依善業的聞、思、修三慧事作比較。聞，就是聽聞佛法；思，學到佛法的知識後，還要不斷複習，一次又一次的思惟，才會產生力量調伏煩惱。所以聞慧與思慧相比，思慧比較殊勝。思及修比，思當然是不如修的。修是實際修止觀斷除煩惱。以聞、思、修相比，修性是最殊勝的。修性無罪，因為修是徹底將心裡的貪瞋癡完全去除。這是依善業來說明業自性，於聞思修及施戒修，這六法作一個比較。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳四、事</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科事，事就是對象，由事使業增上。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">事故者，謂如有一，於佛法僧及隨一種尊重處事，為損為益，名重事業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由所造業對象的重大使業成猛利極重業，是指如有一類人，對於佛法僧三寶，及隨一種應該尊重的對象，如師長或是有德的人、恩田、或敬田、悲田等，於這類對象有損害或利益的作為，名為重事業。這種業通於損益兩方面。對佛法僧特別恭敬，功德也是特別殊勝。佛法不離誠敬，要有誠心要有恭敬。誠信的對象就是三寶，及尊重處事。敬田，對於敬田就應該要尊重，對於悲田就應該要慈悲，對於恩田就應該要報恩，如果能這樣作，生命一定越來越增上。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳五、所治一類</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科所治一類，於所應對治的一類使業增上。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所治一類故者，謂如有一，一向受行諸不善業，乃至壽盡無一時善。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由屬於所應該對治的惡業使業成猛利極重，是指如有一類人，一直是在造作行使種種的不善業，不會因為良心不安，又去造一點善業，因此乃至到壽盡時都沒有作過一些善業，也沒有對治這些惡業，便成斷善根。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="09p649"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳六、所治損害</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科所治損害，所對治的不善業被損害使善業增上。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所治損害故者，謂如有一，斷所對治諸不善業，令諸善業離欲清淨。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由所對治的諸不善業被損害的緣故使善業成猛利極重，是指如有一類人，包括修定或者是修無漏慧者，斷除所要對治的種種不善業，修禪定使令不善業不能現行；修無漏的聖道，能使不善業的種子也永遠斷除，使種種善業成就離欲清淨。有欲就會有不善業，離欲了就沒有這些不善業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅七、業顛倒2　卯一、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科業顛倒，說明業顛倒的現象，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="6199:6376"></a>業顛倒云何？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　業顛倒是什麼？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、釋2　辰一、標列</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科標列，標示列舉出來。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此有三種應知。一、作用顛倒，二、執受顛倒，三、喜樂顛倒。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　業顛倒有三種情況：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、作用顛倒：於造業的作用有錯誤。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、執受顛倒：是指思想上有顛倒。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、喜樂顛倒：這件事不應該有喜樂，不過造業者心裡生起喜樂，這也是一種顛倒。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、隨釋3　巳一、作用顛倒2　午一、舉殺生業道2　未一、於誤殺2　申一、標顛倒</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接著各別解釋，分三科；第一科作用顛倒，說明作用顛倒，又分二科；第一科舉殺生業道，舉出殺生業道，又分二科；第一科於誤殺，於誤殺的作用顛倒，又分二科；第一科標顛倒，標出顛倒。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">作用顛倒者，謂如有一，於餘眾生思欲殺害，誤害餘者。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　作用顛倒這件事，是指如有一類有情，本來想要殺害甲，結果殺害到乙，這是誤殺了，稱為作用顛倒。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、辨相似</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨相似，說明相似的情況。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知此中，雖有殺生，無殺生罪；然有殺生種類、殺生相似同分罪生。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當知道在業的作用顛倒情形下，雖然有殺生，卻是沒有殺生罪；可是有殺生種類、殺生相似的同分罪產生。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》雖有殺生無殺生罪等者：此中殺生，由於餘有情事，彼業現行而得究竟。此業非是圓滿業道所攝，由是說言雖有殺生無殺生罪。然於餘生感得壽量短促彼等流果，由是說有殺生種類殺生相似同分罪生。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這其中的殺生，是由於有其餘有情牽連在內，而殺錯對象，使殺生業現行而得究竟完成。但是所造作的業不是圓滿業道所含攝，由此說是雖然有殺生但沒有殺生罪。然而會在後世生感得壽命短促的等流果，因此說有殺生種類殺生相似的同分罪業產生。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="09p650"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、於非情2　申一、標顛倒</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科於非情，於無情物的作用顛倒，分二科；第一科標顛倒，標出顛倒的情況。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若不誤殺其餘眾生，然於非情加刀杖已，謂我殺生。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果不是誤殺其他有情識的眾生，而是對於無情物施以刀殺杖擊的加害，認為我殺生了。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、辨相似</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨相似，說明相似的情況。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知此中，無有殺生，無殺生罪；然有殺生種類、殺生相似同分罪生。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當知道在這種情形下，並沒有殺害到有情識類的生命，沒有殺生罪；然而是有殺生的種類、殺生相似的同分罪產生。例如有人來警告自己可能會被殺害，就作了一個假人，蓋上棉被，使令那個人來殺的時候，看錯對象，就殺到假人，沒有殺到人。歷史上有這種事情，這種情況也是作用顛倒，殺的對象不對，也是會有殺生種類的同分罪生。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》無有殺生無殺生罪等者：此中加害非實有情，由是說言無有殺生無殺生罪。然於餘生感得外分光澤尠少彼增上果，由是說有殺生種類殺生相似同分罪生。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這其中所傷害的不是真實的有情，因此說沒有殺害到有情識類的生命，沒有殺生罪。然於下一生會感得外分器世間依報光澤尠少的增上果，因此說有殺生種類殺生相似的同分罪產生。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、例不與取等</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例不與取等，例說不與取偷盜等的作用顛倒。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如殺生業道，如是不與取等一切業道，隨其所應，作用顛倒應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同殺生業道的作用顛倒，其他的如不與取等一切不善業道，造業的對象若是錯誤的，隨所對應的作用顛倒業，也是同樣的情況，應該知道。這類業不是得到異熟果，但會得到等流果，或者是增上果的同分罪。對象是有情就得到等流果，對象是無情所得的增上果是依報，這是根據對象是依報或正報來分別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、執受顛倒2　午一、執無罪褔2　未一、標彼立</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科執受顛倒，說明執受顛倒，分二科；第一科執無罪福，執著無罪無福的顛倒，又分二科；第一科標彼立，標出執無罪福者安立的見解與言論。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">執受顛倒者，謂如有一，起如是見，立如是論：無施無受，乃至廣說一切邪見。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　執受顛倒這件事，是指如有一類人生起這樣的見解，安立這樣的言論：布施不能得福，也不能受到好的果報，乃至沒有此世他世，無父無母，無阿羅漢等等的邪見。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、顯彼執</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯彼執，顯示這類人的執著。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="09p651"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼作是執：畢竟無有能殺、所殺，若不與取乃至綺語，亦無施與、受齋、修褔、受學尸羅；由此因緣，無罪無褔。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這類人作這樣的執著：認為畢竟沒有能殺害的人，也沒有所殺害的人，包括不與取的偷盜乃至綺語的惡業也一樣，也沒有布施、受齋、修福、領受學習持戒的福業，於這些事情都撥無的，由這類因緣，執著造惡業無罪，行善業也沒有褔報。這是這類人所執著的邪見。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》畢竟無有能殺所殺等者：此即前業因中彼邪見相應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這就是前面所說業因中的邪見相貌，應該知道。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、執褔無罪2　未一、於殺生</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科執福無罪，執著有福無罪的顛倒，分二科；第一科於殺生，舉出於殺生的顛倒。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又如有一，起如是見，立如是論：若有眾生憎梵、憎天、憎婆羅門。若彼憎惡，唯應殺害。殺彼因緣，唯福無罪。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又如有一類人，生起這樣的見解，安立這樣的言論：如果有眾生憎恨厭惡初禪的大梵天、梵眾天、梵輔天、欲界天人、婆羅門。認為這類心懷憎惡厭惡初禪大梵天等的人，應該將他們殺害，殺死他們的因緣，只有福報沒有罪過，這是一種邪見。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、於不與取等</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科於不與取等，舉出於不與取等不善業的顛倒。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又於彼所起不與取乃至綺語，唯獲福德，無有非福。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又對於這類心懷憎惡的人，去偷盜他們的財物乃至對他們說妄語、惡口、兩舌、綺語等，認為只有福德沒有罪過，這也是錯誤的邪見。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》若有眾生憎梵憎天等者：此即前業因中彼法想相應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這就是前面所說業因中他們所執著為合法想的相貌，應該知道。他們認為合道裡合法的，稱為法想。認為殺自己不喜歡的對象是合法的，這是大邪見。順我者生逆我者亡，這樣的錯誤思想，執福無罪，這是執受顛倒。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、喜樂顛倒</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科喜樂顛倒，說明喜樂顛倒的相貌。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="28438:6404"></a>喜樂顛倒者，謂如有一，不善業道現前行時，如遊戲法，極為喜樂。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　喜樂顛倒這件事，是指如有一類人，在十不善業道現前時，還覺得是在玩弄遊戲法則，極為歡喜快樂，這類人的顛倒是以造惡業為樂。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》喜樂顛倒等者：此即前業因中彼喜樂相應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這即是前面所說業因中這類人所執著喜樂相應的相貌，應該知道。前面業因中曾討論到喜樂相。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是說明業顛倒錯誤的情況。第一種是作用顛倒，是所殺的對象錯誤，或是有情，或是執著對所討厭的對象去傷害他，造作不善業是有福無罪的，這是錯誤的思想。或第三種喜樂顛倒的情況，作十不善業心裡還很高興等。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅八、業差別3　卯一、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科業差別，說明業的差別，分三科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="09p652"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">業差別云何？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　業有各式各樣不同的情況，業的差別是有哪些？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、列2　辰一、體性差別</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列舉出來，分二科；第一科體性差別，說明業的體性差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂有作業，有不作業；有增長業，有不增長業；有故思業，有不故思業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　業的體性差別有：作業、不作業、增長業、不增長業、故思業、不故思業六種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、作業，如下說作業是指若思業，若思已所起身語業。審慮思及決定思名思業，動發思名思已所起身語業。據《大乘阿毘達磨雜集論》卷7說：「作者，謂起造諸業令其現行。」</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、不作業，指若不思惟，任運所造業，或不思惟不起身業、語業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、增長業，如下文說除十種業名增長業。《俱舍論頌疏論本》卷18說：有五因名增長業：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一由審思，審思造業名增長業；率爾思作，但名造作。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二由圓滿，由十惡業具足方墮惡趣，齊墮惡趣，名為圓滿。此圓滿業，名增長業；未圓滿時，但名造作。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三由無惡作對治，造惡不追悔名無惡作，造惡不懺悔洗除，名無對治，這種業名增長；若能追悔，及能悔洗除，但名造作。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四由有伴，指作不善業，以其他不善業為助伴，名增長，如盜他財，復污他室，殺他子等；若無其他不善業助伴，但名造作。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五由有異熟，指造惡業，定感異熟，名增長；不招異熟，但名造作。雖舉惡業為例解釋增長，善業道理也是一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《大乘阿毘達磨雜集論》卷7說：增長，是指令習氣增益，於阿賴耶識中長養異熟種子故。於故思作業若作若增長，重故必定受異熟。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、不增長業，與增長業相反，造業之後不再增長，即下文所說的夢、無故思、不利不數、狂亂所作業、失念所作業、非樂欲、自性無記、悔所損業、對治所損等十種業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、故思造業，《大乘阿毘達磨雜集論》卷7舉出五種故思所造不善業：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（一）他所教敕故思造業，自己雖不想造業，因他人強力之所教敕發起，故思造不善業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（二）他所勸請故思造業，因他人勸請、引導，執為利益，發起故思行不善業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（三）無所了知故思造業者，不了解功德過失，無所執著，隨欲所作，發起故思行不善業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（四）根本執著故思造業，為貪瞋等諸不善根煩惱遮蔽其心，猛利執著，發起故思行不善業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（五）顛倒分別故思造業，依不平等因見愛樂邪法，為求當來可愛異熟，發起故思行不善業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、不故思業，指非故作或非增長名不故思業。故思業當定招感異熟果，不故思業當來不決定招感異熟果。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、種類差別</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科種類差別，說明業的種類差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是定異熟業、不定異熟業，異熟已熟業、異熟未熟業，善業、不善業、無記業，律儀所攝業、不律儀所攝業、非律儀非不律儀所攝業，施性業、戒性業、修性業，褔業、非褔業、不動業，順樂受業、順苦受業、順不苦不樂受業，順現法受業、順生受業、順後受業，過去業、未來業、現在業，欲繫業、色繫業、無色繫業，學業、無學業、非學非無學業，見所斷業、修所斷業、無斷業，黑黑異熟業、白白異熟業、黑白黑白異熟業、非黑非白無異熟業能盡諸業，曲業、穢業、濁業，清淨業、寂靜業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　業的種類共有四十三種，也可以依業的性質要略歸納為十三類：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、異熟：定異熟業、不定異熟業，異熟已熟業、異熟未熟業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、三性：善業、不善業、無記業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、律儀：律儀所攝業、不律儀所攝業、非律儀非不律儀所攝業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、三福：施性業、戒性業、修性業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、三業：褔業、非褔業、不動業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、三受：順樂受業、順苦受業、順不苦不樂受業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七、受果：順現法受業、順生受業、順後受業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　八、三時：過去業、未來業、現在業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　九、三界：欲繫業、色繫業、無色繫業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十、聖果：學業、無學業、非學非無學業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十一、對治：見所斷業、修所斷業、無斷業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十二、黑白：黑黑異熟業、白白異熟業、黑白黑白異熟業、非黑非白無異熟業的無漏業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十三、染淨：曲業、穢業、濁業，清淨業、寂靜業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、釋2　辰一、體性攝3　巳一、作不作業2　午一、作</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，詳細解釋二種差別，分二科；第一科體性攝，業的體性差別所攝，又分三科；第一科作不作業，作業與不作業的體性差別，又分二科；第一科作，說明作業的體性。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">作業者，謂若思業，若思已所起身業、語業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　造作業這件事，是指意識的思心所活動造作的業，及意識的思心所造作後所發起的身業、語業。思有三種，審慮思、決定思、和動發思。審慮思及決定思名思業，動發思已後才能動身發語，稱為思已所起身業、語業。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="09p653"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、不作</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不作，說明不作業的體性。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不作業者，謂若不思業，若不思已不起身業、語業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不作業這件事，是指心裡沒有動機，沒有想要造作的思惟，也沒有生起身業語業，三業沒有造作，即是不造作業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、增長不增長業2　午一、增長4　未一、標簡</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科增長不增長業，說明增長不增長業的體性差別，分二科；第一科增長，增長業的體性差，又分四科；第一科標簡，標示簡除十種非增長業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">增長業者，謂除十種業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　會增長的業，除了下列十種業以外都是增長業。作了業還增長，使業變成極重猛利，罪過變重。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、徵起</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵起，問起。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等為十？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是哪十種業？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、別列</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科別列，各別列舉出來。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、夢所作業，二、無知所作業，</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以下說明十種不增長業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、夢所作業：在作夢當中造業，如在夢中誦經禮佛或靜坐，或者是要作殺生偷盜邪淫等。作夢時心力弱，力量較小，所造的業是不增長的。夢所作業是屬於無記業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、無知所作業：不知道而犯下的過錯，這樣的業也不會增長，因為不是特別去分別而造這種業的。佛法裡面有一種不學無知罪。為什麼會造這樣的業？為什麼做錯事情？不知道，也是一種罪，因為不學，所以無知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》無知所作業者：謂於所作有罪無罪，無有覺慧，無所知故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無知所作的業，指沒有學習佛法的人，對所作的事，是有罪過還是沒有罪過，沒有分別或覺悟的智慧，在無知的情況所作的業，是不增長的。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三、無故思所作業，</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、無故思所作業：不是故意思擇後所作的業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》無故思所作業者：如下不故思業釋應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不是故意、特意，沒有經過詳細思考即造作。有些人造業是想了很久，計畫很久才造作，這是故思所作業。無故思所作業是不增長業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">四、不利不數所作業，</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、不利不數所作業：不是很猛利也不是常常作的業。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="09p654"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》不利不數所作業者：若非上品意樂之所發起，是名不利所作業。及於彼業不樂親近、修習、或多修習，是名不數所作業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在造業時，內心的意樂不是很猛利上品意樂所發起的，稱為不利所作業。及對於所造作的業不是樂於親近的、也不是常修習、或常常多修習的，稱為不數所作業。不論作惡事或作善事，不常常作不會增長，常常作便會增長。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">五、狂亂所作業，</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、狂亂所作業：於心識狂亂時所作的業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》狂亂所作業者：謂由癡狂、心亂、痛惱所逼而有所作故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是指精神有問題，愚痴發狂、心識散亂時、或是有極大的痛苦煩惱逼迫而有所作時，名狂亂所作業。這時所作的業是不會增長，因為這是自己沒辦法控制，等心識清醒後，自己也不知道曾作過什麼事情。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">六、失念所作業，</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、失念所作業：失去正念所作的業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》失念所作業者：謂於有罪雖有覺慧及有所知，而住忘念、住不正知，作不應作故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　聖人對於有罪事，雖然有覺悟的智慧及有所了知，偶而也會有一時忘失正念，住在虛妄分別中、不能正知自己的過失，造作不應作的業。這類短暫、偶失正念、不是故意造的業是不增長業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">七、非樂欲所作業，</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七、非樂欲所作業：不是自己所樂欲作的業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》非樂欲所作業者：謂所作業由他教敕，非自起彼欲樂故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所作業由他人教唆命令去作，不是自己生起欲樂而作的業。這種是不增長業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">八、自性無記業，</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　八、自性無記業：所造業的體性是無記性，不是善也不是惡，這種是不增長業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷3：窺基大師解釋，自性無記業指非業道所攝中下品的善不善業，不是指三性中的無記性，自體不增長故名無記；或三性中無記之業名自性無記業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》自性無記業者：如下無記業釋應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　自性無記業，如下對無記業的解釋應該知道。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">九、悔所損業，</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　九、悔所損業：對所造的業，產生厭惡、後悔及懺悔。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》悔所損業者：謂如造作不善業已，還即如法疾疾悔除，令還淨故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　悔所損業是指如果造作不善業後，能夠如法如理的快速懺悔除遣，使令自己的身語意業回復清淨。快速懺悔所造業，業力會減輕，不會再增長。如果不懺悔，還會繼續造作，業力會越來越增長。懺悔是有用的，懺悔是佛門裡面一種很重要的修行法門。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">十、對治所損業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十、對治所損業：懺悔所造的業對自己對他人有所損害，更進一步修止觀，對治煩惱種子，使煩惱永不起，而永不再造業。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="09p655"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》對治所損業者：謂依世間及出世間諸對治道，或能損伏、或能永害彼彼種故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依止世間及出世間的種種對治道，於修世間禪定的對治道，能損害調伏煩惱種子；若修出世間的對治道，在止觀中修苦集滅道四諦能永遠斷除煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未四、結名</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科結名，結說名增長業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">除此十種，所餘諸業名為增長。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　除了這十種不會增長的業，其餘的業都會增長。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、不增長</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不增長，說明不增長業的體性差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不增長業者，謂即所說十種業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不會增長的業，是指前文所說的十種不增長業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、故思不故思業2　午一、故思</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科故思不故思業，說明故思不故思所造業的體性差別，分二科；第一科故思，說明故思所造業的體性差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">故思業者，謂故思已，若作業、若增長業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　故思業這件事，是經過有意的思惟後，而造作的業、或是由思惟造後再繼續增長的業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　會故意去造這種業或增長這種業，有五種原因：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、他所教敕：他人教導命令自己這樣作。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、他所勸請：不想作，他人勸導自己去這樣作。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、無所了知：不明白功德過失而造業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、根本執著：內心有極重的貪瞋癡，所以去造這種業力。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、顛倒分別：有邪見，所以去造故思業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、不故思</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不故思業，說明不故思業的體性差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不故思業者，謂非故思所作業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不故思業，是指不是故意去思惟後所造作的業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》故思業及不故思業者：謂先思量已，隨尋思已，隨伺察已，而有所作，名故思業。若異此者，即名不故思業。如下攝事分說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/90.htm#6451:68815">陵本九十卷二頁6792</a>）</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　先思惟考量後，又經粗的觀察與仔細的觀察後，才決定有所造作，名為故思業。如果與故思業不同的，不是經過詳細思惟觀察，或是不經意的這樣作，就是不故思業。如下〈攝事分〉卷90，2664頁所說。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="09p656"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、種類攝15　巳一、定不定受業2　午一、順定受</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科種類攝，業的種類差別所攝，分十五科；第一科定不定受業，定不定受業的種類差別，又分二科；第一科順定受，說明順定受業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">順定受業者，謂故思已，若作若增長業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　順定受的業，是經過自己詳細思惟考慮，而造作的故思增長重業，這種決定會受果報。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、順不定受</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科順不定受，說明順不定受業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">順不定受業者，謂故思已，作而不增長業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　順不定受報的業，是指故意思惟以後，有所造作而不增長的輕業。不是重的業，也不再去想，或者業造了以後懺悔；覺得不應該作的，不讓它增長，不一定會受果報。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》順定受業及順不定受業者：謂由此業定受彼果，是名順定受業。又所作業不定受果，是名順不定受業。又順定受業，謂故思所造重業。不定受業，謂故思所造輕業，如下攝事分說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/90.htm#6457:68827">陵本九十卷二頁6793</a>）</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　造了這種業，一定受相應於業的果報，稱為順定受業。如果所造的業，不一定受果報，稱為不定受業。又順定受業，是故意思惟後所造的重業。不定受業，是故意思惟後所造的輕業。如下〈攝事分〉卷90，2665頁所說。《大乘阿毘達磨雜集論》卷7說定受業有三種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、作業決定，由宿世的業力感得決定異熟相續，在這一生中必定造此業。這是因為應造這種業的期限是決定的緣故，終究不會超越期限，決定造這種業，乃至諸佛世尊大神通力，也不能障礙令他不造。這是隨因中的決定力，得果時相續轉變故。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、受異熟決定者，如先所說故思造業若作若增長。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、分位決定者，指現法受等前際、中際、後際分位決定業。例如由這種業於現法中必定受異熟果成順現法受業，由這種業必受生異熟成順生受，由這種業必受後異熟成順後受等差別。（受異熟決定只是說決定受果，分位決定在說明業在前際、中際、後際的差別，此文依原文所舉）。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、已熟未熟業2　午一、異熟已熟</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科已熟未熟業，說明已熟業及未熟業的種類差別，分二科；第一科異熟已熟，說明異熟已熟業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">異熟已熟業者，謂已與果業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　經過異時、異類、變異成熟的業，是指已得果報的業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、異熟未熟</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科異熟未熟業，說明異熟未熟業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">異熟未熟業者，謂未與果業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　異熟未熟業，是指尚未感得果報的業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、善等性業3　午一、善</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科善等性業，善等性業的種類差別，分三科；第一科善，說明善業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">善業者，謂無貪、無瞋、無癡為因緣業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　善業，是指以無貪、無瞋、無癡為因緣所造的業。例如布施、持戒、忍辱、精進、禪定、般若等，施、戒、修都是善業。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="09p657"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、不善</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不善業，說明不善業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不善業者，謂貪瞋癡為因緣業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不善業，是指以貪瞋癡為因緣所造的業。例如十惡業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、無記</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科無記業，說明無記業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">無記業者，謂非無貪、無瞋、無癡為因緣，亦非貪瞋癡為因緣業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無記業，是指造業時，不是以無貪、無瞋、無癡為因緣，也不是以貪瞋癡為因緣所造的業。這種業不會受果，例如以無記心作一些工巧的事等。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳四、律儀等攝業3　午一、律儀所攝</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科律儀等攝業，說明律儀等所攝業的種類差別，分三科；第一科律儀所攝，說明律儀所攝業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">律儀所攝業者，謂或別解脫律儀所攝業，或靜慮等至果斷律儀所攝業，或無漏律儀所攝業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　律儀所攝的業，指別解脫律儀所攝業、或靜慮等至果斷律儀所攝業，或無漏律儀所攝業。律儀有三種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、別解脫律儀又名別解脫戒，佛教七眾弟子，發起出離心後，經過一定的儀式，誓願受持佛所制七眾戒的某一種，七眾戒包括比丘戒、比丘尼戒、式叉摩那戒、沙彌戒、沙彌尼戒、優婆塞戒、優婆夷戒，在記憶裡留下深刻的印象（在阿賴耶識中熏成種子），以後遇緣對境，會有防止惡行的作用，名為別解脫戒。其中由出家者盡形壽遠離惡行欲行受比丘戒等，由近事者盡形壽離惡行不離欲行受五戒，由近住者不能盡形壽離惡行欲行受八關齋戒，因此別解脫戒又分三類建立。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、靜慮律儀，也名定共戒，由定力壓伏煩惱而不犯戒。靜慮是指心在極靜的狀態下又能夠思惟，由此證得四種靜慮；等至即是平等能至，是指心能安住在平等、捨受的地方，證得空無邊處、識無邊處、無所有處、還有非想非非想處的四空定。四禪及四空定的果，可以斷除欲的煩惱，稱為果斷律儀。果是約靜慮的果及等至的果合起來說的，這種戒稱為定共戒。這是依有漏定生戒的道理而說。〈決擇分〉說：唯色界有定共戒，此文及下列第三分文通無色定有，《大乘阿毘達磨集論》等唯依色界建立，該論說因為無色界粗色無故，略不建立定共戒。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、無漏律儀，也名道共戒，由智慧力斷除煩惱而不犯戒，證無漏聖道才有。這是三乘聖者，證入出世間無漏定時與無漏智共於身中自發得防非止惡之戒體（即無漏之律儀），稱為無漏律儀。又此無漏之律儀，與無漏道共生，與無漏道共滅，因此名道共戒。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》律儀所攝業等者：七眾所受律儀戒，是名別解脫律儀。依止靜慮及諸等至，伏斷現行諸煩惱纏，是名靜慮等至果斷律儀。證諦現觀，爾時一切能往惡趣惡戒種子皆悉永害，是名無漏律儀。攝決擇分廣辯應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/53.htm#6471:40994">陵本五十三卷五頁4222</a>）</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　比丘、比丘尼、式叉摩那又稱學法女、沙彌、沙彌尼、優婆塞、優婆夷等七眾所受的律儀戒，稱為別解脫律儀。依止靜慮禪定及四空定諸等至，能伏斷煩惱的現行，但沒有斷除煩惱種子。稱為靜慮等至果斷律儀，又名定共戒。證得四諦現量觀察的無分別智時，心是無分別的狀態，這時在阿賴耶識中，能使令到三惡道去的一切惡戒的種子全部斷除，稱為無漏律儀，又名道共戒。如決擇〈五識身相應地意地〉卷53，1749頁所說。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、不律儀所攝3　未一、標</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不律儀所攝，說明不律儀所攝，分三科；第一科標，標出十二種。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不律儀所攝業者，謂十二種不律儀類所攝諸業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不律儀所攝的業，是指十二種不律儀類所攝的諸業。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="09p658"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等十二不律儀類？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是哪十二種不律儀類？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、列</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科列，列舉出十二種。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、屠羊，二、販雞，三、販豬，四、捕鳥，五、罝兔，六、盜賊，七、魁膾，八、守獄，九、讒剌，十、斷獄，十一、縛象，十二、呪龍。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有十二種是不律儀，皆是與惡法相應的業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、屠羊：為活命故懷殺害心，包括買羊、賣羊、養羊、殺羊這一切都屬殺羊種類的不律儀。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、販雞：為活命故懷殺害心，包括買雞、賣雞、養雞、殺雞這一切都屬殺雞種類的不律儀。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、販豬：為活命故懷殺害心，包括買豬、賣豬、養豬、殺豬這一切都屬殺豬種類的不律儀。四、捕鳥：為活命故採捕眾鳥等類。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、罝兔：為活命故在山上放一些網子來捕兔子等類。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、盜賊：常行劫奪及偷竊財物的人是不律儀。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七、魁膾：以殺人為職業的劊子手，在監獄裡面負責將人處決掉的，這種職業也是不律儀。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　八、守獄：以顧守監獄自活的人。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　九、讒刺：唯行讒儜譏刺於他以求活命者，是專門寫文章找他人缺點或是用媒體來宣傳他人的缺點者。《成實論》卷10說：以瞋恚心無畏敬心侵惱善人，名讒刺。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十、斷獄：是指法官之類的官員，能判決犯人的入獄刑期。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十一、縛象：首陀羅等為活命故縛象維生者。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十二、呪龍：首陀羅等為活命故習呪術來指揮龍，有說龍也通於蛇，有一種職業是以耍龍弄蛇維生。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、非律儀非不律儀所攝</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科非律儀非不律儀所攝，說明非律儀非不律儀所攝業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">非律儀非不律儀所攝業者，謂除三種律儀業及不律儀類業，所餘一切善、不善、無記業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　屬於非律儀非不律儀所攝的業，除了別解脫戒、定共戒及道共戒這三種律儀業，以及十二種不律儀類業以外，其他的善業、不善業或無記業，稱為非律儀非不律儀所攝業。這種既非律儀之極善，也非不律儀之極惡，而是隨緣應時而生起的善惡；即處中之善與處中之惡，這種善、惡之勢用微劣，因此稱為處中之善惡；並不是戒律之善與惡，其體不生善或不善。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《大乘阿毘達磨雜集論》卷8說：「所有善、不善業，若布施、愛語等業，若毆擊等業，律儀、不律儀所不攝，名非律儀非不律儀。」</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳五、施等性業2　午一、約法相辨2　未一、舉施性2　申一、標列</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科施等性業，說明施等性業的種類差別，分二科；第一科約法相辨，依法相說明，又分二科，第一科舉施性，舉布施的特性，又分二科；第一科標列，標示列舉出布施的種類差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">施性業者，謂若因緣、若等起、若依處、若自性。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以布施為體性的業，性也可以通於心，凡有布施心來造的業，通稱施性業，包括布施的因緣指發動布施的心念，布施等起指能捨所施物及能起身語業思，布施的依止處是指施物及對象，布施的自性指布施的身語二業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、隨釋4　酉一、因緣</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接著分別解釋，分四科；第一科因緣，說明布施的因緣。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼因緣者，謂以無貪、無瞋、無癡為因緣。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　布施的因緣，是以沒有貪、瞋、癡的心情為因緣。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、等起</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科等起，說明布施的等起即施相應思。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="09p659"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼等起者，謂無貪、無瞋、無癡俱行，能捨所施物、能起身語業思。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　布施的等起，是指心與無貪、無瞋、無癡在一起活動，因此生起能施捨所施的物品，如錢財或是體力等，及能發起身語業的思心所即動發思。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》彼等起等者：此中文應長讀。當知體即是思。謂由此思，能捨所施物，能起身語業，如是故名能捨所施物能起身語業思。此思與無貪、無瞋、無癡俱時現行，是名無貪、無瞋、無癡俱行。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這其中的文應該要將它讀完，才能了解它的意思。應當知道等起的體性是思心所，因為有這種思心所的活動，而能布施財物，能夠生起這類的身業及語業，因此名為能捨所施物，能起身語業思。布施的思心所是與無貪無瞋無癡三種善心所同時在一起活動，稱為無貪無瞋無癡俱行。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉三、依處</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科依處，說明布施的依處。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼依處者，謂以所施物及受者為依處。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　布施的依處，是指以所布施的物品，包括金銀錢財等無情物、有情的人或是家畜等，及接受布施的對象為依止處。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》彼依處等者：當知此中有情數物、無情數物，一切總說名所施物。於有苦者、或有恩者、或親愛者、或尊勝者，是其所施，一切總說名為受者。如下聲聞地說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/25.htm#6491:21007">陵本二十五卷十四頁2128</a>）</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當知道這其中布施的有情數物及無情數物，一切總說名為所施物。對於有苦難的人去救濟他，有恩的人去報答他，親愛的人去供養他，尊勝的人是三寶的處所，或者是值得尊敬、特別有道德的人，去作種種的布施，這些都是接受布施的對象。如下〈聲聞地〉卷25，875頁所說。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉四、自性</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科自性，說明布施的自性。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼自性者，謂思所起能捨所施物身業、語業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　布施的自性，是指由動發思所起能施捨所施物的身業及語業。大乘包括意業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、例戒性等2　申一、標隨應</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例戒性等，例舉戒性等的種類差別，分二科；第一科標隨應，標出隨順其所相應的種類。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如施性業，如是戒性業、修性業隨其所應應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同施性業是分這四點來說，戒性業與修性業隨其所相應也分四點來說明。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="09p660"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、釋差別2　酉一、戒性2　戌一、指同</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋差別，解釋其中的差別，分二科；第一科戒性，說明戒性的種類差別，又分二科；第一科指同，指出因緣、等起同前。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中戒性業，因緣、等起如前。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其中戒性業的因緣與等起，如同前施性業所說。戒性業以無貪無瞋無癡為因緣，等起就是無貪無瞋無癡俱行的能受淨戒及能持淨戒的身語業思。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、顯別2　亥一、自性</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯別，顯示差別的地方，分二科；第一科自性，說明戒的自性。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">自性者，謂律儀所攝身語業等。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　戒性業的自性，是指律儀所攝的身業語業等。律儀即是戒，行者的身業語業是有持戒的，稱為戒性業。聲聞戒重點在身業語業。菩薩戒則動念便犯戒，這裡的等是包括意業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、依處</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科依處，說明戒的依處。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依處者，謂有情、非有情數物。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　戒性業的依處，是指有情數物、非有情數物。例如一般說持不殺生的別解脫戒，不可以傷害有情，以有情為依處；持不偷盜戒，不可以偷盜他人的財物，是以非有情數為依處。總之持戒的依止處包括有情及非有情數物。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、修性4　戌一、因緣</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科修性，說明修性的種類差別，分四科；第一科因緣，說明修性的因緣。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">修性因緣者，謂三摩地因緣，即無貪、無瞋、無癡。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　修性的因緣，是指三摩地（禪定）的因緣，便是無貪、無瞋、無癡。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、等起</span></strong></span></span>
