<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於業無知是什麼？是指對於各式各樣的業，生起不合道理的分別，認為有造作業的作者所有的無知。業有福業、非福業、及不動業，福業是欲界的善業，非福業是造作當來會到三惡道受報的十惡業，不動業，修當來能感色無色界天的色無色界定。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄八、於異熟無知</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科於異熟無知，說明於異熟無知的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於異熟無知云何？謂於異熟果所攝諸行起不如理分別，謂有受者所有無知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於異熟無知是什麼？是指對由業而生的異熟果所攝的五蘊諸行生起不如理的分別，認為是有一個受者在受此果報的所有無知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄九、於業異熟無知</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科於業異熟無知，說明於業異熟無知的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於業異熟無知云何？謂於業及果起不如理分別所有無知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於業異熟無知是什麼？是指對於所造業與感得果之間的關係，生起不如理分別的所有無知。不知道善因得善果、惡因得惡果，受持五戒可以當人，造十善業可以生到欲界天，造不動的禪定業可以生到色無色界天。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於業無知於異熟無知於業異熟無知者：諸業謂因，異熟謂果，因果相屬名業異熟。若於諸業唯有行性不能了知，而妄計度我為作者，是名於業無知。若於一切世間業因所起，妄計自在、作者、生者，而更計我為其受者，名於異熟無知。或更於業及果不能了知相應道理，妄興誹謗一切都無，是名於業異熟無知。由是因緣，於生天等非正處中起妄勝解，歸依敬信；當知此非處信，即是業等無知所生。是故建立此三差別。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　諸所造作的業就是因，所變異成熟的就是果，因與果之間是有相屬關係的，造如是因得如是果，名為業異熟。如果對於業的造作唯是遷流不息、無常變異的諸行性不能正確的了知，而虛妄的計度有一個我在那裡造作，我為作者，這樣的無明名為於業無知。如果對於一切世間是由業因的造作而生起，卻虛妄的計度有一個主宰性的大自在天神為作者、或另有一位造作者、或是能生果者，而更加計度執著我是其中的受者，名為於異熟無知。或是更對於業因與業果之間的關係不能知道其中因與果的相應道理，善業得到樂果，惡業得到苦果，這是有相應的，但是不明白。而虛妄的興起誹謗，撥無一切因果，名為於業異熟無知。由於這樣的因緣，對於生到天上或人間等不是正確的解脫及離雜染處，生起虛妄的勝解，而去皈依及敬信天神，不知道要皈依三寶。應該知道這是不合道理的信仰，這就是對業、異熟、業異熟的無知所產生的結果，因此建立這三種差別。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="09p707"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄十、於佛無知</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十科於佛無知，說明於佛無知的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於佛無知云何？謂於佛菩提，或不思惟、或邪思惟、或由放逸、或由疑惑、或由毀謗所有無知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於佛的無知是什麼？是指對於佛的覺悟智慧，或是不思惟、或是有邪執的思惟、或是由於有放逸、是或由於有疑惑、或是由於有毀謗的所有無知。阿耨多羅三藐三菩提這是佛弟子們所追求的。菩提是斷除煩惱、所知二障以後所得的智慧。玅境長老開示，菩提有二種，一種是如理智、一種如量智。如理智就是根本無分別智，如量智就是後得無分別智。如理智是實智，如量智是權（方便）智。如理智可以斷除一切煩惱，如量智知道一切緣起法的智慧，而且對一切所知的蘊界處，世間、出世間的事情都能通達無礙。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛的智慧在〈菩薩地〉卷38與卷49那裡也會很詳細的說明。「或不思惟」，對於佛成就的菩提因為沒有聞思的智慧不知道是什麼，就不去思惟；「或邪思惟」，或者他有成見想錯了，或者他學錯了；「或由放逸」，或是放縱自己在五欲當中享受五欲，不能精進的斷惡生善，深入經藏，而不知什麼是佛；「或由疑惑」，或由於沒有深入的聞思修，對於佛成就的菩提，如何成就的菩薩道等產生疑惑，不能有決定的勝解；「或由毀謗」，或是外道對於佛法有成見而毀謗，或是執著二乘為究竟者，只相信阿羅漢，認為大乘非佛說，而毀謗大乘佛法，以上這些都是一種於佛的無知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄十一、於法無知</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十一科於法無知，說明於法無知的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於法無知云何？謂於正法善說性，或不思惟、或邪思惟、或由放逸、或由疑惑、或由毀謗所有無知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於法的無知是什麼？是指對於佛所說正法的初善、中善、後善的善說性，沒有深刻的思惟觀察、或是有邪執的思惟、或是由於放逸、或是有種種的疑惑、或是有毀謗正法過失的所有無知。善說性的初善，是說於初聽佛法時能令人歡喜，因為它能掃除內心的煩惱；中善，聽了佛法後，中間用來修行時沒有障礙，也沒有艱苦而且是中道而行，遠離二邊；後善，依著佛所說的法來修行，將來一定是成就無上菩提，或者是成就涅槃。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　法有世俗正法與勝義正法二種，世俗正法是指由語言文字安立的經律論，勝義正法是依世俗正法修出世聖道證得無分別智時才能通達的第一義諦。「或不思惟」，或對於正法沒有學習無法思惟，或雖然有學習正法卻懶得去想它，或深刻的思惟觀察；「或邪思惟」，或者想錯了；「或由放逸」，或不努力學習佛法，心遊蕩在五欲上面；「或由疑惑」，或者學得不夠仔細不能決定，所以對於法也有種種的疑惑；「或由毀謗」，或者毀謗正法等；若對於世俗正法不能思惟乃至毀謗，不僅於世俗正法不能勝解更不可能通達勝義正法，這些都是對於法的無知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄十二、於僧無知</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十二科於僧無知，說明於僧無知的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於僧無知云何？謂於僧正行，或不思惟、或邪思惟、或由放逸、或由疑惑、或由毀謗所有無知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於僧的無知是什麼？是說對出家眾的正行，應該要如何正確的修行，或是沒有深刻的思惟觀察、或是有邪執的思惟、或是由於放逸、或是有種種的疑惑、或是有毀謗僧過失的所有無知。僧，梵語僧伽，中國說為和合眾，指出家三乘之人，其心與佛所說事理之法和合，因此名僧。要達到事和與理和，必需透過三乘的戒定慧等正行，若於三乘的正行不能思惟；或邪思惟，有錯誤顛倒的思惟；或是放縱自己的身口意於五欲上；或是於三乘正行有所懷疑、迷惑；乃至或由毀謗三乘正行，這些都是對於僧的無知。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="09p708"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於佛無知於法無知於僧無知者：二斷、二智，名佛菩提。如下菩薩地釋。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/38.htm#6940:30668">陵本三十八卷一頁3097</a>）聽聞正法，初中後善，是名正法善說性。如下異門分釋。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/83.htm#6940:63521">陵本八十三卷十二頁6312</a>）文巧義妙，故名善說。若應理行，若質直行，若和敬行，若隨法行，如是差別名僧正行。又自然覺悟相名佛菩提，覺悟果相名正法善說性，隨他所教正修行相名僧正行，由是建立三寶差別，所謂佛寶、法寶、僧寶。於此三寶所有功德不生敬信，是名無知。如是無知，或由不思惟起，聞說功德不了義故；或由邪思惟起，於所聽聞不善領悟故；或由放逸故起，耽著諸欲，不樂親近故；或由疑惑故起，不生勝解，無淨信故；或由毀謗故起，住自見取，誹謗功德故；由此無知，能生一切外道邪見，是故建立此三差別。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二斷指煩惱障斷、所知障斷，二智指一切煩惱不隨縛智及於一切所知無礙無障智，得到這二種智慧，名為佛菩提。如下〈菩薩地〉卷38，1255頁所說。聽聞正法的初中後善，名為正法善說性。如〈攝異門分〉卷83，2498頁所解釋。佛所說的法文字與義理是非常的巧妙深細，名為善說。僧，出家眾的正行，包括如理如法的應理行：依止聖教，無諂無誑，如實顯現教理的純樸正直的質直行；僧團和合的六和敬行；隨三十七道品正法修行的隨法行，這些差別名為僧的正行。又以另一種說法，佛在菩提樹下無師自悟，自然覺悟相名為佛菩提；佛覺悟的成果相名為正法善說性，由此能善巧的教化導引眾生；隨佛所教導的，能正確的依戒定慧教法的修行相，名為僧正行；由此建立三寶的差別，所謂佛寶、法寶、僧寶；若對佛法僧三寶不生恭敬的信心，名為無知。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這些種種的無知，或是由於不作思惟所引起的，這是因為聽聞所說的三寶功德不明白其中義理的緣故；或是由於有邪執的思惟生起，這是因為對於所聽聞的法義不能善為領納悟入的緣故；或是由於放逸散亂所引起，這是因為耽著在諸欲的欲樂中，而不歡喜愛樂親近正法的緣故；或是由於疑惑生起，這是因為對於佛法不能深入學習，不能生起勝解，沒有清淨信心的緣故；或是由於執著自己錯誤的成見而毀謗三寶，安住在自己偏執的見取中，而誹謗三寶的功德；由於這種種的無知，能生起一切的外道邪見，因此建立對佛法僧無知的三種差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄十三、於苦等無知2　黃一、舉於苦諦</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十三科於苦等無知，說明於苦等無知的差別，分二科；第一科舉於苦諦，舉出於苦諦無知的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於苦無知云何？謂於苦是苦性，或不思惟、或邪思惟、或由放逸、或由疑惑、或由毀謗所有無知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於苦諦的無知是什麼？是指對於苦是有苦的體性，沒有深刻的思惟觀察或不思惟；或是有邪執的思惟，錯誤而顛倒的思惟；或是由於放逸，放縱自己的身口意於五欲中、或是有種種的疑惑，對於苦諦沒有勝解、淨信，內心懷疑迷惑；或是有毀謗苦諦的所有無知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、例於集等</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例於集等，例舉出於集諦、滅諦、道諦等無知的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如於苦，當知於集、滅、道無知亦爾。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同於苦諦，應當知道對於集諦、滅諦、道諦的無知也是一樣。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="09p709"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於苦無知等者：苦集滅道，是為四諦。謂苦為真苦，集為真集，滅為真滅，道為真道，義無虛妄，唯聖所證，故名為諦。無始時來理成就性，法爾無諍，名苦性等。苦是染果，集是染因，滅是淨果，道是淨因，於如是等不能了知，是名於四無知。此亦能生一切邪見，是故建立此四差別。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　苦集滅道，是佛陀所教導修習出世間法的四種真實的諦理。經由如實的依聖教修行，可以真實的體驗苦真實是苦，五蘊苦果真實是苦；集真實是集，愛見煩惱真實是集聚苦的因；滅真實是滅，涅槃是苦和集的寂滅是真實清淨的；道真實是道，八正道真實是能證得清淨的聖道，四諦的義理沒有任何虛假不實，唯有聖人能親身體證，所以名為諦理。無始以來這些道理成就的法性，自然是如此而沒有諍論，名為苦性等。苦是雜染的果，集是雜染的因，滅是清淨的果，道是清淨的因，對於這些不能正確的了知，名為於四諦無知。因為這種種的無知能生出一切的邪見，因此佛陀建立這四種諦理的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄十四、於因等無知2　黃一、辨因果2　宇一、舉於因</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十四科於因等無知，說明於因等無知的差別，分二科；第一科辨因果，說明因果無知的差別，又分二科；第一科舉於因，舉於因無知的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="48761:6948"></a><a name="11529:6948"></a>於因無知云何？謂起不如理分別，或計無因，或計自在、世性、士夫、中間等不平等因所有無知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於因的無知是什麼？這是對於宇宙萬有的生起，包括生命體還有器世間，所生起的原因有種種的無明，而生起不如理的分別。或者是執著有情及器世間都是無因而有的；或者是計度執著有情是大自在天所生的、所創造的，但是大自在天是誰創造的？他是無因而有的。世性，也稱為冥性，就是外道入定時，只能觀察到八萬大劫的事，八萬大劫以外的事看不到了，稱為冥性。由於不了解，認為有一個不可思議的冥性生出世間的萬有，冥性還沒有創造宇宙萬有稱為自性，已經創造宇宙萬有稱為世性。或者是有一類人主張是士夫，就是常恒住、不變異、有主宰性的神我來創造有情的生命體與器世間。還有中間等，就是初禪二禪的中間定的大梵天王，由大梵天王創造宇宙萬有。總之外道執著宇宙萬有是由自在、世性、士夫、中間等所創作，而這些創作者本身卻是無因而有的，是自然法爾而有的，這類執著他作我受果的不平等因論等對於萬法生因所有的無知，稱為於因無知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宇二、例於從因所生諸行</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例於從因所生諸行，例說於從因所生的諸行無知的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如於因無知，於從因所生諸行亦爾。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同對於因的無知，對於從因所生的五蘊諸行的無知也是一樣。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於因無知等者：自身緣起是名為因，緣生諸行是名為果。若於緣起妄計為無，是名無因論者。或復計餘為因而不稱理，是名不平等因論者。如是二計，若於因起，是名於因無知；若於果起，是名於因所生諸行無知。由是道理，故言亦爾。妄計諸行無因而生，或不平等因之所起故，由此能生生天方便增上慢，是故建立此二無知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　緣起是名為因，由緣所生的色受想行識是名為果。如果對於緣起錯誤計為是沒有的，是名無因論者。或又執著是其他不如理的因來創造生命體，例如生命體是由自在、世性、士夫、或中間等所創造，是名不平等因論者。如此二種錯誤計度執著，如果是由因而生起的，名為於因無知；如果是由果而生起的，名為由因所生諸行的無知。於因無知則於果必然也無知，所以說亦爾。若錯誤認定五蘊果非緣起而生的，或者是不平等因所生起的，則能夠產生錯誤的生天方法，如以殺害羊等為生天的因，或誤以生天為究竟涅槃等增上慢，因此建立於因無知及於因所生諸行無知這二種無知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、廣染淨</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣染淨，詳細說明染差別。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="09p710"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="16743:6954"></a>又彼無罪故名善，有罪故名不善；有利益故名應修習，無利益故名不應修習；黑故名有罪，白故名無罪；雜故名有分。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又彼，是指因與從因所生諸行，包括因與果，因與果如果是沒有罪過的，就是屬於善法，有罪過的名為不善；有利益的緣故，因此名應該修習，無利益的緣故，因此名不應修習；因是黑的，如十惡業，果也是黑的，如三惡道，因此名為有罪；因是白的，如十善業，果也是白的，如三善道，因此名為無罪；因中黑白夾雜，如善中惡、惡中善，造業時心有染淨二分，三業也有善惡夾雜，果中黑白夾雜，如人中得黑白黑白異熟等，因果都是黑白夾雜名為有分。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》又彼無罪故名善等者：此顯前二染淨種類差別，皆彼無知所攝，與緣起經開合有別，故唯說有十九種無知。此中雜故名有分者，謂黑白分間雜而有，故名有分。如說黑白黑白異熟業是。餘文易知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡顯示前二染淨種類差別，就是於因無知及從因所生諸行的無知，對因果這二種的染淨種類差別，都是屬於無明所攝的，在《緣起經》裏面開演得比較廣，這裡只有說十九種無知，二種說法有差別。這其中有黑白相雜，所以名為有分，是指黑白區分間雜而有，因此稱為有分，就是造業時有黑有白，白時就是無罪的，黑時就是有罪過的。例如因是有黑有白的，果也是有黑有白的，這種黑白黑白異熟業前面說過。其他的文就容易懂了。在〈決擇分〉中還會再說到這件事情。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄十五、於六觸處如實通達無知</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十五科於六觸處如實通達無知，對於六觸處如實通達無知的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於六觸處如實通達無知云何？謂增上慢者，於所證中顛倒思惟所有無知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於六觸處如實通達的無知是什麼？是說增上慢者，未得上聖之法，自謂已得，未證上聖之理，自謂已證，對於自己所證的境界中有顛倒錯誤思惟的所有無知。佛在《中阿含經》卷42說到眼觸見色，耳觸聞聲，鼻觸嗅香，舌觸嘗味，身觸覺觸，意觸知法名六觸處，由此六觸處，根境相觸時內心有喜憂捨三受，由此產生貪瞋癡三種煩惱，而有六喜觀、六憂觀、六捨觀等十八意行，佛為此說六觸處。若修行人於所證的禪定功德，暫伏煩惱，根境相觸時相似清淨，誤以為聖道稱為增上慢。佛弟子一定要深入學習佛法，才能免除增上慢。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、結</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結，結說名十九種無知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是略說十九種無知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如上所說要略而言有十九種無明，包括前際、後際、前後際、於內、於外、於內外、於業、異熟、業異熟、於佛法僧三寶、於苦集滅道四諦、於因、於果（從因所生諸行）、六觸處如實通達等無知，說得非常詳細。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="09p711"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於六觸處如實通達無知等者：六觸處者，謂眼等根名為六處，緣觸生時，名六觸處。若於其時無明相應，無明為緣便生於行、行緣識等，由是能引生死苦果。若於其時無明不起，爾時與觸俱生六處，雖緣六境而不生染，彼無明因永滅寂靜，便無緣行、行緣識等，如實通達沙門果證，如是名為於六觸處如實通達。於此所證若未通達，妄自顛倒，謂已通達，是名於六觸處如實通達無知。此中無知能生沙門果增上慢，是故建立。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　眼耳鼻舌身意六根稱為六處，依六根觸對色聲香味觸法時，名為六觸處。如果接觸境界有無明相應時，以無明為緣，就會產生福等三種業行，由行緣識等，在阿賴耶識中熏習了識名色六入觸受五法種子，由此能引未來的生死苦果。如果六根接觸六境時沒有無明生起，那時與觸同時生起的六根，雖然緣取六境，由於有如理作意，而不會有貪瞋癡煩惱相應所生起的染著，由於無明的因永遠斷滅而寂靜，就不會有無明緣行、也不會有福行、非福行、不動行去緣識等，不會再熏習三界的種子，將來也不會在三界裏引出苦果，已經如實的通達沙門果證，如是名為於六觸處如實通達。如果對於自己所證得的境界，還沒有通達，而虛妄執著自己錯誤顛倒的認知，認為已經通達，是名於六觸處如實通達的無知。這其中的無知，能生起對沙門果未證為證的增上慢，因此建立於六觸處如實通達的無知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、七種無知2　地一、總標列</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科七種無知，說明七種無知的差別，將前面的十九種無知歸納成七種無知說明，分二科；第一科總標列，總相標示列舉出來。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="43321:6963"></a>復有七種無知。一、世愚，二、事愚，三、移轉愚，四、最勝愚，五、真實愚，六、染淨愚，七、增上慢愚。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有七種無知。世愚、事愚、移轉愚、最勝愚、真實愚、染淨愚、增上慢愚。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七種無知的要義：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、世愚：對於過去、現在、未來三世到底有沒有我這件事，有愚癡有無明。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、事愚：對色受想行識五蘊的內身、外境、其他有情等有無明。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、移轉愚：於因緣所生的有為法等業果移轉有無明。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、最勝愚：對於最殊勝的三寶不明白其義。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、真實愚：對於真實苦集滅道是一切法的真理，染淨因果的實相，不明白及無知。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、染淨愚：對於因無知及於因所生諸行的染淨，是有罪無罪？有利益無利益？應修習不應修習？黑或是白？或者是黑白夾雜？這件事情不明白。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七、增上慢愚：是對於六觸處如實通達不明白，有未證謂證的增上慢的無明。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、別明攝2　玄一、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別明攝，各別說明十九種及七種無知互相含攝，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">前十九無知，今七無知，相攝云何？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前面十九種無明和現在七種無明，它們相攝的情況是如何？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、釋</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂初三無知攝初一，次三無知攝第二，次三無知攝第三，次三無知攝第四，次四無知攝第五，次二無知攝第六，後一無知攝第七。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前面三種：前際無知、後際無知、前後際無知，攝於世愚。第二組三種無知：於內無知、於外無知、於內外無知，攝於事愚。第三組三種無知：業無知、異熟無知、業異熟無知，攝於移轉愚。第四組三種無知：對於佛法僧三寶無知，攝於最勝愚。第五組四種無知：對於苦集滅道四諦無知，攝於真實愚。第六組二種無知的：能生因，及因所生諸行無知，攝於染淨愚。最後一種無知：於六觸處如實通達無知，攝於增上慢愚。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》復有七種無知等者：愚三際故，此名世愚；愚內外俱，此名事愚；愚業果俱，名移轉愚；愚三寶故，名最勝愚；愚四諦故，名真實愚；愚能生因及所生法，名染淨愚；愚沙門果證，名增上慢愚。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　愚於前際、後際、前後際無我的道理，名為世愚。愚於內身、外境、及內身外境無我的道理，名為事愚。愚於業、異熟、業異熟的道理，名為移轉愚。愚於佛法僧三寶的道理，名為最勝愚。愚於苦集滅道四諦的道理，名為真實愚。愚於創造宇宙萬有的能生因以及從因所生五蘊諸行等果法，名為染淨愚。愚於初果、二果、三果、四果的證得體相，名為增上慢愚。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="09p712"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天三、五種愚2　地一、總標列</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科五種愚，說明五種愚的差別，將十九種無明及七種無明再歸納為五種說明，分二科；第一科總標列，總相標示列出五種愚。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="7587:6971"></a><a name="51271:6971"></a>復有五種愚。一、義愚，二、見愚，三、放逸愚，四、真實義愚，五、增上慢愚。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有義愚、見愚、放逸愚、真實義愚、增上慢愚這五種愚。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、義愚：義就是境界，對所有的境界有愚癡，應該包括十九種無知都在裡面，十九種無知都是義愚。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、見愚：思想上有種種的我見等，這種錯誤思想的愚癡包括於前際無知到內外無知六種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、放逸愚：對於業、異熟、業異熟無知，想要有好的境界，又不要作有道德的事情。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、真實義愚：對於三寶、四諦真實的事理有所愚癡。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、增上慢愚：對於聖道沙門果證不了解，就是增上慢愚，這是最後一種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其中見愚還包括對於因無知，因為它包括無因論、斷見論、及不平等因論等；第十七種及第十八種從因所生諸行無知，也是屬於見愚。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、明別攝2　玄一、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明別攝，各別說明十九愚及五種愚互相含攝的配對，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">前十九愚，今五種愚，相攝云何？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前面的十九種愚和現在的五種愚，彼此相攝的情況是如何？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、釋</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂見愚攝前六及於因所生法無知；放逸愚攝於業、異熟、俱無知；真實義愚攝於佛等乃至道諦無知；增上慢愚攝最後無知；當知義愚通攝一切。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　見愚含攝：於前際、後際、前後際、於內、於外、於內外前六種的無知，及於因、於果（於因所生法）的無知；放逸愚含攝：於業、於異熟、於業異熟的俱無知；真實義愚含攝：於佛法僧三寶、於苦集滅道四諦的無知；增上慢愚含攝：最後於六觸處如實通達的無知；應當知道義愚通攝一切的十九種無知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》復有五種愚等者：愚於一切所知境界，是名義愚；邪解為依，推求分別，是名見愚；希求生天，不修正行，名放逸愚；不正通達三寶、四諦，是名真實義愚；顛倒妄計得沙門果，是名增上慢愚。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　愚於一切所應該要認識的緣起的境界，稱為義愚；外道以錯誤的理解為依止，錯誤的推斷、尋求、及分別，名為見愚；想要生天去享受快樂，不修佛法的戒定慧，名為放逸愚；對於三寶、四諦的道理沒有正確的通達，名為真實義愚；對得到沙門果，有錯誤的認識與執著，名為增上慢愚。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是約所知事辨，約所認識的色受想行識等境界來說明無明有種種的差別，有十九種無明、七種無明、及五種無明。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、約能知智辨2　天一、異門差別2　地一、辨差別</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約能知智辨，約能知的智慧來說明無明的差別，分二科；第一科異門差別，以不同的角度說明差別，又分二科，第一科辨差別，說明無明的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="09p713"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，無知、無見、無有現觀、黑闇、愚癡，及無明闇，如是六種無明差別，隨前所說七無知事次第應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，無知、無見、無有現觀、黑闇、愚癡，及無明闇，這六種無明的差別，隨前面所說的七種無知事的次第應該知道。也就是無知配世愚；無見是事愚；無有現觀是移轉愚；黑闇是最勝愚；愚癡是真實愚；無明闇是染淨愚及增上慢愚。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、顯總合</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯總合，顯示將後二無知事總合為一。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於後二無知事總合為一，起此最後無明黑闇。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　將後二的染淨愚和增上慢愚合起來的無知事總合為一，就是最後的無明黑闇。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》復次無知無見等者：若於不現見法不能了知，是名無知。若於現見現在前法不能了知，是名無見。若於不由他緣自實所證不能了知，名無現觀。於其實事不正了知，是名黑闇。於不實事妄生增益，是名愚癡。於所知事不能善巧，是名無明。成就誹謗一切邪見，是名為闇。如下異門分說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/84.htm#6982:64699">陵本八十四卷二十頁6413</a>）今於此中，無明及闇總合為一，故言六種。如其次第配七無知，義應準釋。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於現前看不到的法不能明白，名為無知。例如對於過去、現在、未來都是無我的不能了知根本就沒有我，找不到這個我。對於若於現見現在眼前的法不能了知，如內身、外境、其他有情等已經在眼前了，卻不能了解無我，稱為無見。對於不由他緣，需要自己如實所體證的，不能了知，名為無現觀。得到無分別的智慧與真理相應，稱為現觀，沒有現觀的人，對於業、異熟、業異熟的事情不知道。對於三寶等真實的事情不能正確了知稱為黑闇。對不真實的事情虛妄的增益為實，稱為愚癡。這是對於苦集滅道四諦不明白，換句話說是執著常樂我淨，因為四諦就是在說明五蘊無常苦空無我，若於不實的五蘊執著是真實常樂我淨，虛妄的增益不實事為實，稱為愚癡。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於所知道的境界不能善巧，稱為無明，這是對於因無知，及從因所生諸行的五蘊等不能善巧。若毀謗一切三寶、四諦，乃至毀謗真實事，毀謗沙門果，稱為闇。如下〈攝異門分〉卷84，2529頁也有解釋這一段文。現在這裡將無明與闇合起來成為無明闇，所以說有六種，如它的次第配七種無知，義理應準照這裡的解釋可知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、所治差別2　地一、辨2　玄一、約三慧辨</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科所治差別，約所對治的差別來說明無明的差別，分二科；第一科辨，約三慧、三品辨明，又分二科；第一科約三慧辨，以聞思修三慧說明。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有差別。謂聞思修所成三慧所治差別，如其次第說前三種。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　還有差別。是說聞思修所成的三慧所對治的差別，如於前後際等無知的世愚可用聞所成慧對治、於內外等無知的事愚可用思所成慧對治、於業異熟等無知的移轉愚可用修所成慧對治，以這樣的次第說前三種。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、約三品辨</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約三品辨，約三品說明。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">即此所治軟中上品差別，說後三種。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是約所對治的無明有軟中上品，軟品是對於三寶的無知，是比較輕微的；中品是對於四諦的無知；上品是後三種對於因無知乃至六觸處如實通達無知，是這樣配合起來說。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="09p714"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、結</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結，結說六種無明差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是所治差別故，自性差別故，建立六種差別應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　根據以聞思修慧所對治的無明差別、自性差別，來建立無知、無見、無有現觀、黑闇、愚癡及無明闇六種無明差別應該知道。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》復有差別等者：聞慧所治說名無知，思慧所治說名無見，修慧所治說無現觀，此約所治差別建立前三；軟品無明說名黑闇，中品無明說名愚癡，上品無明說無明闇，此約自性差別建立後三；如是總有六種差別應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　聞慧所對治的說名無知，思慧所對治的說名無見，修慧所治的說為無現觀，這是約所對治的差別建立前三種；軟品的對三寶無明說名為黑闇，中品的對四諦無明說名為愚癡，上品的對於因等及果（從因所生諸行）的無明說為無明闇，這是約無明自性的差別建立軟中上品的後三種。這樣總共有六種差別應該知道。這是以所對治的煩惱，與能對治的智慧來說明的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上解釋無明差別，有十九種無知、七種無知、五種愚、六種無明的不同分類與異名。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、行差別3　亥一、身行3　天一、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科行差別，說明行的差別，分三科；第一科身行，說明身行的差別，又分三科，第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">身行云何？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　身行是什麼？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、標</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科標，標出來。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂身業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　就是身業，身體的活動。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天三、辨</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科辨，說明。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若欲界、若色界，在下名福非福，在上名不動。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　身行，是指身業，身體的活動稱為身行。如果是在欲界或者是色界，欲界是在下地，稱為福、非福行，色界在上地，稱為不動行。因為無色界沒有身體，此處未說，事實上無色界善業也是不動行。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="09p715"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》身行云何等者：入出息風，名為身行。風為導首，身業轉故。身所作業，亦名身行。由愚癡者先起隨順身業風已，然後方起染汙身業。如下決擇分說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/56.htm#6998:44820">陵本五十六卷十八頁4552</a>）今說身行，謂即身業，其義應知。又此身業唯欲色界有，是故說言若欲界、若色界，不通無色界，以無所依身故。若在欲界，所起身業感五趣生，是故彼業名福非福。若在色界，定地所攝，是故彼業名為不動。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有入息風、有出息風，名為身行。以風為前導發動，身業即能隨轉活動，身體能動是因為有風，風是以流動為性。身所造作的業行，也名為身行。例如身體造作的殺盜淫妄事情，都稱為身行。有無明的愚癡凡夫，要先生起隨順身業的風後，才能去造作染汙的身業。如下〈決擇‧五識身相應地意地〉卷56，1865頁所說。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　現在所說的身行就是身業，道理應該要了解。又這種身業，只有欲界及色界的人有，因此說若欲界、若色界，不通於無色界，因為無色界的眾生沒有所依止的色身。在欲界所起的身業，所造的福業或非福業，能感得五趣受生，福業能到人天，非福業能到三惡道去。如果是色界，是屬於定地所攝，所以這種業稱為不動業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、語行3　天一、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科語行，說明語行的差別，分三科，第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">語行云何？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　語行是什麼？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、標</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科標，標出語行的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂語業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　語行是指語業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天三、辨</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科辨，說明語行的種類。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">餘如前應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其餘語行的業如前所說應該知道，在欲界就是福非福業，上二界異熟果無語行，名不動業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》語行云何等者：尋伺相應，是名語行。由此為先，語業隨轉，故說語行謂即語業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　能夠說話，是由於名為先故想，想為先故說，心裡要有粗的思惟觀察的尋，也有細的思惟觀察的伺，才能夠說出一句話，通常是有想過才能說話，沒有想沒有尋伺，是不能說出一句話。例如看到一棵樹，一定有想到這是樹，才能夠說出來，尋伺相應，名為語行。要先經過尋伺的思惟觀察然後才能夠說話，所以說語行就是語業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥三、意行3　天一、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科意行，說明意行的差別，分三科；第一科徵，提問</span></span></span></div>
<a name="09p716"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">意行云何？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　意行是什麼？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、標</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科標，標出意行的體性。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂意業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是指意業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天三、辨</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科辨，說明意行的種類。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若在欲界名福非福，在上二界唯名不動。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果在欲界的意業，不外是善行及不善行，福業及非福業。如果上二界的色、無色界定稱為不動行。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》意行云何等者：受想相應，是名意行。由此為先，意業方轉，是故此說謂即意業。色無色界皆定地攝，故說彼業唯名不動。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　意行主要是內心有受，有感受，有想相應，名為意行。先有受有想，然後才能夠有意業活動，因此說這就是意業。色無色界都是屬於定地所攝，所以說上二界的業唯是名為不動。通常意行也不能離開思心所，有思心所，才能夠造業，才會有意行。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、識差別2　亥一、辨相2　天一、舉眼識2　地一、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科識差別，說明識的差別，分二科；第一科辨相，說明識的相狀，又分二科；第一科舉眼識，舉出眼識說明，又分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">眼識云何？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　眼識是什麼？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、釋</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂於當來依止眼根了別色境識，所有褔、非褔、不動行所熏發種子識，及彼種子所生果識。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　眼識是什麼呢？就是對將來能夠依止眼根了別色境的識，包括欲界的福、非福行，及色無色界的不動行所熏發的種子識，以及這些種子所生的果識，眼識種子產生現行，得到果報，也是眼識。總之包括眼識種子與眼識現行，名眼識。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、例餘識2　地一、例同</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例餘識，例舉出其餘的識，分二科；第一科例同，例說相同的。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="09p717"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如眼識，如是乃至意識應知亦爾。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同眼識，如是耳鼻舌身識及意識也是一樣，依止意根了別法境識，所有福、非福、不動行所熏發種子識，及彼種子所生果識，包括諸識種子與諸識現行。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、顯別</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯別，顯示六識的所依及境界的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由所依及境界，所起了別差別應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由所依止的根及所緣的境界，所生起識的了別差別應該知道。眼識是依止眼根，耳識是依止耳根，乃至意識是依止意根，識所依止的根，還有根所緣的色聲香味觸法境，由此根境不同所生起的識的了別也有所差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由所依及境界所起了別差別應知者：所依謂眼等六根，境界謂色等六境，了別差別謂眼等六識。此結前說眼識乃至意識得名應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　眼等識所依止的是眼耳鼻舌身意等六根，境界是色聲香味觸法等六境，了別的差別是指眼耳鼻舌身意等六識；眼耳鼻舌身五識都是只能現前了別與剎那了別，唯意識能相續了別與進一步分別。這裡的結前，是說眼識乃至意識所得到的名稱都包括種子與現行，應該知道。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、料簡</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科料簡，再詳細的思惟簡擇識的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此於欲界具足六種，色界唯四，無色界唯一。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這在欲界有眼識耳識鼻識舌識身識意識六種。在色界沒有鼻識與舌識，因為沒有段食不用嗅香與嚐味，在無色界只有一種，即是意識。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》此於欲界具足六種等者：欲界具有眼等六識。色界除鼻舌識，唯有餘四。無色界除眼等五，唯一意識。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲界具有眼等六識。色界除了鼻舌識，只剩下眼耳身意識四種，無色界只有一種意識。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌四、名色差別2　亥一、別辨種類2　天一、名差別2　地一、辨相4　玄一、受蘊</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科名色差別，說明名色的差別，分二科；第一科別辨種類，各別說明名色的種類，又分二科；第一科名差別，說明名的差別，又分二科；第一科辨相，說明名的相狀，又分四科；第一科受蘊，說明受蘊的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">受蘊云何？謂一切領納種類。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　受蘊是什麼？是領納一切境界的種類，都可以稱為受蘊。蘊就是積聚，有各式各樣的受，眼等五識有苦、樂、捨三受，意識有苦、樂、憂、喜、捨受五受相應，第七識及第八識唯捨受相應。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、想蘊</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科想蘊，說明想蘊的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">想蘊云何？謂一切了像種類。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　想蘊是什麼？是說一切了像種類。想可以取相，稱為想。心怎麼能想，因為心接觸色聲香味觸法，一定有一個相貌，例如若想到某甲，心就有一個某甲的相貌。想有小想、大想、無量想、無所有想，欲界繫想名為「小」；色界繫想名為「大」；二無色天繫想名為「無量」；無所有處繫想是名「無所有想」。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="09p718"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄三、行蘊</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科行蘊，說明行蘊的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">行蘊云何？謂一切心所造作意業種類。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行蘊是什麼？是指一切心所造作意業的種類。心的造作，主要是思心所，稱為行蘊。此處行主要指意行，或福、非福、不動行。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄四、識蘊</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科識蘊，說明識蘊的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">識蘊云何？謂一切了別種類。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　識蘊是什麼？是指所有了別的種類都可以稱為識蘊，包括眼等六識，及第七末那識、第八阿賴耶蘊。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、料簡</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科料簡，重新思惟簡擇名蘊的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是諸蘊皆通三界。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這受想行識四種蘊都是通於欲界、色界、無色界，三界眾生都有。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》受蘊云何至皆通三界者：受謂領納，想謂了相，行謂造作，識謂了別，此說四蘊自相差別。為顯蘊義，故說彼彼一切種類，由一類總略義是蘊義故。如是四蘊皆通三界。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　受是領納順違俱非境相為性，想是於境了相為性，行是令心造作為性，識是於境了別為性，這是說四種蘊的自相差別。為了顯示蘊的義理，因此說這些蘊的一切種類，由彙集為一類總義或略義是蘊義的緣故。這四種蘊都通於三界的。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、色差別2　地一、四大種2　玄一、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科色差別，說明色蘊的差別，分二科；第一科四大種，說明地、水、火、風的差別，又分二科，第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">四大種云何？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四大種是哪些？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、釋2　黃一、出體</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科出體，說出四大的體性。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂地、水、火、風界。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是說地是以堅為性，水是以濕為性，火是以暖為性，風是以動為性。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="09p719"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、料簡</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科料簡，重新思惟簡擇四大的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此皆通二界。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　地、水、火、風四大都通於欲界、色界，此二界才有色法，無色界的天人沒有。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、所造色2　玄一、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科所造色，說明所造色的差別，分二科，第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">四大種所造色云何？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四大種所造色是什麼？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、釋2　黃一、出體</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科出體，說出所造色的體性。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂十色處及法處所攝色。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是指十色處的眼耳鼻舌身色聲香味觸，及法處所攝的律儀色、不律儀色、三摩地所行境色。眼等五根，還有色等五境，稱為十色處。法處所攝色，在這裡只說出三種，包括律儀色，不律儀色，及三摩地所行境色。律儀色就是去受戒時，在三皈依，乃至羯摩，或是戒師在說戒相時，都很專心在聽，就會領納到心裡，熏成業種子，稱為律儀色，這是無表色，不是真實的色，是假安立的。不律儀色，是指不防護身語業者，由彼增上造作惡業的心心法故；依彼所現行的身語惡法，建立色性假法。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三摩地所行境色，名定自在所生色，又作定所生色、定所引色、勝定果色、定果色、自在所生色；即指由禪定力所變現之色聲香味等境；此類色法係以勝定力於一切色變現自在，故稱定自在所生色。又此類色法通於凡聖所變，然凡聖所變現者有假實之別，若由凡夫之禪定力所變現者，為假色，不能實用；若由八地以上之聖者，憑威德之勝定力，能變現為可實用之實在色法，例如變土砂而成金銀魚米，可令有情眾生受用之，是實色，這是在心力很強的禪定裡面，所現出來的色，是有作用的。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、料簡</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科料簡，重新思惟簡擇所造色的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">欲界具十及法處所攝假色；色界有八及法處所攝色，然非一切。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲界具有眼耳鼻舌身，色聲香味觸十色，法處所攝色的假色。色界有眼耳鼻舌身、色聲觸八種，色界的人也有眼耳鼻舌身根，因為色界已無段食，沒有香與味；色界也有法處所攝色，包括律儀色，及三摩地所行境色，但不是一切，色界沒有不律儀色，生到四種禪天的人，不會再造惡業。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="09p720"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂十色處及法處所攝色等者：眼等五根，色等五境，名十色處。若一切時意所行境，色蘊所攝，無見無對，是名法處所攝色。此復三種，謂律儀色、不律儀色，及三摩地所行境色。（如顯揚一卷十三頁釋）初二假有，後一實有。於欲界中具十色處，及有律儀、不律儀色，是故說有法處所攝假色。於色界中，十色處除香味二，故唯有八；法處所攝色有三摩地所行境色及律儀色，無不律儀，故非一切。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　眼耳鼻舌身等五根，色聲香味觸等五境，名為十色處。於一切時意識所緣色的境界，雖是屬於色蘊所攝，但卻是肉眼看不見也沒有質礙的，是名法處所攝色。意識所緣的境界是法塵，所以其中所攝的色蘊部分，安立名為法處所攝色。這裡說到三種：律儀色，是指善戒體（善思種子）；不律儀色（指現行惡身語），及三摩地所行色。如《顯揚聖教論》卷1，13頁所解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前二種的律儀色及不律儀色，是假有的，不是真實的色法，後面的三摩地所行色有假實差別，如後面〈決擇‧五識身相應地意地〉卷53，1757頁說的滅盡定亦是假有，非實物有。在欲界中具有的十色處，及有律儀、不律儀色，因此說有法處所攝的假色。在色界中，十色處除去香味二種色法，因此只有八種色法。法處所攝色中有三摩地所行境色、及律儀色，但沒有不律儀色，所以不是一切的法處所攝色。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、總釋體性</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科總釋體性，總相解釋名色的體性。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此亦二種。謂識種子所攝受種子名色，及於彼所生果名色。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　名色的體性也有二種，就是識種子所攝受種子的名色（識種子所攝受名色種子），以及名色種子所生果（識種子所攝受名色現行）：在母胎裡已經現行出來的名色。總之包括名色種子及現行名色，都是名色。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》此亦二種等者：此謂名色亦如六識說有二種，謂種子名色，及彼種子所生果名色。此種子名色隨逐於識，由是說言為識種子之所攝受。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡是說名色也如同六識說有二種，包括種子的名色，及種子所生果的名色。這些種子的名色隨逐於阿賴耶識，因此說為識種子之所攝受。依大乘的道理，種子的名色在第八識中，如果是聲聞乘經部的解釋，在根、根依及識中。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌五、六處差別3　亥一、辨相2　天一、舉眼處2　地一、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科六處差別，說明六處的差別，分三科；第一科辨相，說明六處的相貌，又分二科；第一科舉眼處，舉出眼處的差別，又分二科，第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">眼處云何？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　眼處是什麼？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、釋</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂眼識所依淨色，由此於色已見、現見、當見。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　眼指眼根，處是什麼？〈決擇‧五識身相應地意地〉卷56說，諸心心所生長門義、緣義、方便義、和合性義、所依止義、居住處義，是名處義。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　眼處是指眼識所依的清淨色：眼根，有眼根才能夠發出眼識，依止眼根於色境已見到，是指過去；現見，是指現在；當見，是指未來。換言之，過去現在未來都能夠發出眼識緣著色境。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、例餘處2　地一、標隨應</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例餘處，例舉其他的耳鼻舌身意五處也是一樣，分二科；第一科標隨應，標示出隨所相應處。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如眼處，如是乃至意處，隨其所應盡當知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同眼處是這樣，耳處、鼻處、舌處、身處，乃至意處，隨它所相應的都應該知道。例如耳處是耳識所依淨色，由此於聲已聞、現聞、當聞；意識的所依是意根，它不是清淨色根，是無色法，由此意根於法已了、現了、當了，其餘諸識所相應的，由前推理應當可以完全了知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、例差別</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例差別，例說三時業用差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於一切處，應說三時業用差別。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在六處中，約依根發識取境，應該說明取境時有過去、現在、未來時間的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="09p721"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、出體</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科出體，說明六處差別的體性。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此亦二種。謂名色種子所攝受種子六處，及彼所生果六處。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六處的差別也是有二種，是指名色種子所攝受的種子六處，及六處的種子所生的果報（現行）六處。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥三、料簡</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科料簡，詳細思惟簡擇六處差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">五在欲色界，第六通三界。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六處中的五處是眼耳鼻舌身，在欲界及色界中有，第六就是意處，意處通於三界，欲界、色界、無色界都有。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由此於色已見現見當見者：此顯眼處於一切時恆為眼識所依，故說於色已見、現見、當見。唯恆所依為定量故，說心心所名有所依。如下決擇分說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/55.htm#7070:43100">陵本五十五卷四頁4403</a>）餘一切處說三時別，準此應釋。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是顯示眼根於一切時恆常為眼識所依止，因此說於色過去已見、現前見到、未來將會見到。由於根能為識恆常所依止，以此事實為量（標準），說心心所名為有所依。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如下〈決擇‧五識身相應地意地〉卷55，1812頁所說。其餘一切處如耳處乃至意處其業用含括過去現在未來三時差別，準照此處道理解釋。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌六、觸差別3　亥一、辨相2　天一、舉眼觸2　地一、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科觸差別，說明觸的差別，分三科；第一科辨相，說明觸的相貌，又分二科；第一科舉眼觸，舉出眼觸，又分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">眼觸云何？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　眼觸是什麼？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、釋</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂三和所生，能取境界淨妙等義。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　根境識三和合會生起觸，由此能取得境界的淨妙、非淨妙及非淨妙非非淨妙的境界。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、例餘觸</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例餘觸，例舉出其餘諸觸。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是餘觸，各隨別境說相應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其他的耳觸等也都是三和所生，能取境界淨妙等義，各自隨其所相應的應當了知。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="09p722"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、出體</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科出體，說明觸的體性。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此復二種。謂六處種子所攝受種子觸，及彼所生果觸。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六觸也包括二種觸，是指六處種子所攝受的種子觸，以及六處種子現行的果觸，現在接觸到境界的都是屬於果觸。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》眼觸云何等者：眼所生觸，是名眼觸。當知此觸非唯眼生，根境識三和合生故；眼根依勝，得眼觸名。由此取境，成三差別，若好、若惡、若二俱非，似色顯現，由是說言能取境界淨妙等義。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　眼所生觸，名為眼觸。應該知道這種觸不是只由眼根所生，是由眼根、色境、眼識三和合所生的；因為觸生中眼根依最有勝用，所以得到眼觸的名稱。眼觸取著境界，成為好、惡、非好非惡的三種差別。所取的觸境，都是眼識五遍行心所中之觸種子所變現，相似真實的色法而顯現，不是色法而是心所法所現相分，所以稱為似色顯現，能取境界的清淨美好微妙等義。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥三、料簡</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科料簡，思惟簡擇觸的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">欲界具六，色界四，無色界一。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲界具有眼耳鼻舌身意六種觸，色界有眼耳身意四種觸，無色界只有一種意觸。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》欲界具六等者：眼等六觸，欲界全，色界闕無鼻舌二觸，無色界唯有意觸應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲界的人一定有眼耳鼻舌身意等六觸，色界因為沒有段食，所以沒有鼻觸及舌觸，無色界的天人只有意觸。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌七、受差別3　亥一、辨相3　天一、樂受</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科受差別，說明受的差別，分三科；第一科辨相，說明受的相狀，又分三科；第一科樂受，說明樂受的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">樂受云何？謂順樂諸根、境界為緣，所生適悅受，受所攝。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　樂受是什麼？就是隨順生起樂受的六根，六境為緣，發出六識時，所生的舒適愉悅的感受，及此受所攝的身心。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、苦受</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科苦受，說明苦受的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">苦受云何？謂順苦二為緣，所生非適悅受，受所攝。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　苦受是什麼？是說隨順苦的諸根與境界二法為緣，所生的不是適悅的受，及此受所攝的身心。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="09p723"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天三、不苦不樂受</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科不苦不樂受，說明不苦不樂受的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不苦不樂受云何？謂順不苦不樂二為緣，所生非適悅非不適悅受，受所攝。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不苦不樂受是什麼？是指隨順不苦不樂的諸根與境界，以這二種為緣所生的不是苦的受，也不是快樂的受，及此受所攝的身心。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》樂受苦受不苦不樂受者：此中三受由三所顯，謂受因緣、受自性，及受所攝。受因緣者，謂順樂、順苦，及順不苦不樂諸根境界。受自性者，謂適悅受、非適悅受、非適悅非不適悅受。受所攝者，謂適悅受、非適悅受、非適悅非不適悅受所攝身心。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這其中三種受是由三種所顯現，這三種是受的因緣、受的自性，及受所含攝的身心。受的因緣會產生受，是指隨順生起樂受、隨順生起苦受、及隨順生起不苦不樂受的六根與六境。受的體性，包括：適悅受、非適悅受、非適悅非不適悅受，就是樂受、苦受、和不苦不樂受。受所攝，是指適悅受、非適悅受、非適悅非不適悅受所攝的身與心的領納狀態</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、料簡</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科料簡，再詳細簡擇受的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">欲界三，色界二，第四靜慮以上乃至非想非非想處唯有第三不苦不樂。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三界有情的受方面，欲界有樂受、苦受、不苦不樂受三種；色界只有樂受及不苦不樂受二種，沒有苦受，因為初禪二禪三禪都有樂受，第四禪以上到無色界的最高天非想非非想處天，都只有不苦不樂受。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥三、出體</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科出體，說明受的體性。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此亦二種。謂觸種子所攝受種子受，及彼所生果受。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　受的體性也有二種狀態，一是觸種子所攝受的種子受即受種子，及受種子所生的果受，即現行的苦受、樂受及不苦不樂受等。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》欲界三色界二等者：於色界中，前三靜慮有樂受及不苦不樂受，唯無苦受，是故言二。餘文易知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在色界中，前三禪當中有樂受及不苦不樂受，只是沒有苦受，所以稱為二種，其他的文應該容易明白。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">瑜伽師地論科句披尋記卷第九</span></strong></span></span>
